settings screen. \r\nSupported image formats include JPEG, PNG, GIF (including animated GIFs), BMP, TIFF and many RAW formats including DNG.\r\nA Pro version upgrade is available as an in-app purchase - this includes a thumbnail view and transition effects. The Pro upgrade is also required to play videos, and supports many common video formats, including files with extensions mp4, m4v,mkv, mts, m2ts, avi, mov, wmv, mpg, mpeg and mpe (but support also depends on the encoding used within these files). For mpg and mpeg files you may need to download the free MPEG-2 Video Extension (by Microsoft) from the Store.\r\n\r\n(Note RAW format support depends on the camera model.
